\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00022}00022 \textcolor{comment}{    *** Remaining Flags ***}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00023}00023 \textcolor{comment}{    BIG\_MOLECULES -\/ Allow loading molecules with over 99999 atoms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00024}00024 \textcolor{comment}{    SERIAL -\/ Run the program on a single thread (no MPI)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00025}00025 \textcolor{comment}{    REALTIME -\/ Slow down the simulation and incrase frame dumping rate to visualize growth}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00026}00026 \textcolor{comment}{    MACROMODE -\/ Mode when the classes are mostly used from DNV-\/Macro functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00027}00027 \textcolor{comment}{    FRAGGROW -\/ Allow growth using fragments also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00028}00028 \textcolor{comment}{    PLACEHOLDERMOLECULES -\/ Molecules are just placeholders for collections of atoms -\/ Useful to perform analytics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00029}00029 \textcolor{comment}{    NOINTERFACE -\/ No Y/N/O interface when writing out files (deprecated)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00030}00030 \textcolor{comment}{    NOZMQ -\/ Switch off ZMQ library linkage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00031}00031 \textcolor{comment}{    NOJSON -\/ Switch off LibJSoN Support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Molecule_8hpp_source_l00032}00032 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
